< Text>
One of my favorite restaurants. I feel at home here and I'm not sure why. Maybe because the food is very comforting for me. I've tried almost everything on their menu and don't really have anything to complain about. My favorite dishes are the mussels, the pate (which they don't have anymore), the cavatelli, the wagyu ribeye steak, and the slow roasted lamb neck. They change some items on their menu time to time but I'd wish they bring back the pate. It's always busy here so I highly recommend making a reservation weeks in advance, or even months in advance if you're looking for a specific time and date.<//Text>

< review>
A friend invited me to lunch this week here and it was fantastic. We arrived just in time to order the lunch specials, served til 3:00pm. I ordered the cheese pizza with their house salad. Steven the waiter greeted us with warm bread, whuch they make daily, and served with oil and balsamic vinegar. I believe the cook waits for the diners to finish their starters before cooking the entrees, keen eye. I was starving and are all my salad and cheese pizza. The best part is yet to come, when Steven brings over the most delicious Spumoni ice cream I've ever tasted, and made in house. Wow!!! Parking is in back of restaurant and they do have outside dining of you like. Lunch specials were priced low so 2 people could eat for around $25. Great place on Montana that serves awesome Italian food with great employees and say hello to the owner, he's usually around.< /review>

(Translated by Google) Very cozy, clean restaurant with starched textile napkins on the tables, freshly baked aromatic bread and impeccable service. Plus the presence of a good wine list and delicious Italian beer.
Excellently prepared food gives a good cook who knows a lot about Italian cuisine. Prices are above average.
However, you can eat inexpensively during lunch hours: a hearty business lunch starts at $ 11.
The restaurant is very popular with locals. Often at the entrance you can see a long line of visitors of a very respectable appearance who want to attest to their presence in this institution. And this fact is perhaps the best evidence of the success of the restaurant.
If you couldn‚Äôt sit down at one of the cozy tables, do not despair! The restaurant has home delivery service. As they say, any whim for your money. Enjoy!

< Review>
We contracted with Terminix in Gardena to do a tenting service to rid the house of termite infestation. The first person who came out did an estimate, and we looked at other companies, too. We chose Terminix. The next person who came out was overly aggressive and demanded full payment in advance, which we were not comfortable with. We called the office and they sent Travis Wilson to continue the process. At first, he was thorough and nice. He did another estimate that included things we didn't want to do. We scheduled the treatment.
A roofing inspection was done before the treatment, and there were only 8 damaged tiles. It was then that we discovered that Terminix does NOT do the actually tenting, it's done by a company called PEST. They were not careful removing the tarps, and when a follow-up roof inspection was done, they had damaged 89 tiles. We paid for insurance to repair up to 45 tiles, but this was excessive. And now, Travis is no longer with the company and we're getting the runaround. We will probably have to take PEST to small claims court, because Terminix has mandatory arbitration. DO NOT USE TERMINIX FOR TERMITE SERVICE. Terrible experience.</Review>

<rating>4</rating><Review>Tikka Bowl is a fantastic take on Indian-Greek-American fusion. They make amazing food and provide a unique menu that really puts them ahead of the curve. I was surprised with their offerings in terms of the depth and breadth of the menu as well as how good the food was. All of the food I had was made to order and not put on the grill or pulled out of the cold table until it was being prepped for my order.

There are 2 reasons why they don't get 5 stars. The first is that I came about 45 minutes before closing and it was clear that they tried to prep as little as possible for my order, including squeezing a sauce bottle to death and skimping on sauce so they wouldn't have to make more/refill it. Secondly, all of the ingredients looked and tasted fresh except the lettuce which I watched them pull out of a pre-mixed bag. As good as the shawarma style lamb was, it couldn't mask the pesticide tasting, low effort lettuce they topped my naan tacos with.

With little effort, they could take Tikka Bowl to a 5 star experience and I thin this place has crazy potential.

Pictured below is an example of how they can really shine. These are tikka masala paneer fries. They were absolutely amazing.</Review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOpmIiv4TOXj8TQahvQKfNuPq0skq2uWdItVjg-=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics><response>None< /response><gmapID>0x80c34a1bbc70264d:0x152e6a8ef911034<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>

< review>
Nice apartments, great floor-plans, brilliantly accessible to all sorts of stuff, from BART, to Lake Elizabeth, Kaiser medical facilities, COSTCO...it's a fantastic location. Monika (Leasing Agent) was fantastic showing us around the complex, answering all of our questions honestly, and with lots of context. Incredibly affordable ($2,650) 2-bedroom / 2 bathroom units with Washer/Dryer in unit...NO JOKE...WASHER / DRYER IN UNIT! This is insane for the bay area. Fremont is a great city, to boot. For those of you who are reading the negative reviews, make sure you take into account the items being brought up. Getting towed, paying late fees, appliances breaking down...this is what happens in apartment buildings all across the nation. I've yet to speak to anyone who has lived at The Presidio who said that their work orders for maintenance were never fulfilled, or that their neighbors were overly loud or rude, or that the management team was unreasonable. It an apartment complex, for Christ's sake. There are rules and regulations. You also live above and below families and people with all sorts of quirks and habits. If you don't like some of the noises you hear after 8am and before 10pm, then maybe buy a house in the middle of a forest.

***UPDATE - 3/25/2021 ***

We had our first interaction with the maintenance team today. They did not disappoint. They responded quickly to our requests, and were thorough in their service. 3 of the 4 initial items we discovered during our move-in were simply due to a lack of understanding with how the appliances worked or what light-switches controlled what outlets. The other cosmetic issue we requested service on was documented and scheduled for repair quickly. Santos Castro, our maintenance rep helped me understand how our apartment functions without making me feel stupid, even though I admitted as much...that I was stupid...because I was. Overall, he was excellent, helpful, and if he's any indication of the kind of support the maintenance crew typically provides, then they're a good crew.<//review>

I lived in Presidio for about 4.5 years and I should say I have a very pleasant experience. First and prime most, the apartment is a very safe community. It is a gated one, unlike most others in Fremont. The management team led by Mohammed are all wonderful, esp. Marisol, Jayne, and Mark who is not working there now. The management often conducts parties for Christmas/Summer/etc. The swimming pools are great, with an indoor one too. There is a play area now that small kids enjoy. It's a lively place to live in. It get's a little bit louder near the play area so I would suggest to take a look at all the available units and choose the one if you want a quiet unit. The apartment units are getting renovations and they look more beautiful now with newer appliances and hardwood flooring. Keep in mind there will be issues in the community like any other communities. But you can request for a service request on the phone or by calling them, and they are attended immediately for emergency issues. There is an after hours emergency line too. The maintenance staff, Jose, Mario, and all the others are also very nice people. I would highly recommend anyone to this apartment community in Fremont.< /text>

<Text>I grew up in Humboldt and came back in August for my father's funeral. I went to McKinleyville Office Supply in the hopes of supporting a local business and fulfilling my father's service related needs (Printing service announcements ect.). I came in to the store 5-10 minutes before the store closed and the young girl behind the counter made a snarky comment about how everyone wanted to come into the store right before it closed. I ignored the comment because I understand having a long day at work. I asked her if they carried any vellum and she said "yes." I then had to ask her where to find it. Instead of taking me to where the vellum was located, she pointed in a general direction. I generally don't mind finding things on my own but I thought for someone in such a hurry to close the store, she would have shown me where it was so the it would expedite me leaving. It turned out they didn't actually have vellum so I left and went to Michael's. I returned the next day to have a picture and quote printed on (proper) vellum. An older man, Im assuming the owner, refused to print on the paper and said that he didn't think his printer would print on it. When I asked if he would be willing to try printing on one sheet, he flat out refused and got angry with me and offered no other alternative. He told me that he was not going to break his $40,000 printer by trying to print on vellum. (You can print on vellum from a home computer. This experience was so embarrassing and unprofessional that I am writing this review a month later. I ended up going to Scrapper's Edge in Eureka! <Rate>5< /Rate><Text>My husband and I wanted to try a few new places in the Pasadena area, and while walking around, we came across a sign on the Main Street, saying there were coffee and plants in the back. We are both crazy coffee nuts, and we have travelled the world (Germany, Armenia, Dubai, Greece, several states) looking for great coffee shops. This place easily makes the top 5 list. Easily.

I‚Äôm not a fan of non dairy options, so when the owner, AC, told us everything was dairy free, I was worried I wouldn‚Äôt like the taste. He recommended trying oat milk, because it‚Äôs the closest to dairy options. My husband got a cappuccino with almond milk, and I got myself an oat milk 24k chocolate latte.

We also bought a cute little Coffee & Plants pin, something to take home, and I wanted to spend more money in the cafe.

< review>
This place was aesthetically pleasing. I was really excited to try their blue latte based on pictures of other reviews. I ordered it with oat milk and even though it was really pretty to look at, taste wise it disappointed me. The taste was really bland and not worth my money. Beware this drink is non-caffeniated so that is also another strike for me. I would have rated this place higher if it wasn't for the owner's sarcasm. My order had already been placed and he approached us asking if we were from Pasadena etc. As we were talking I noticed they had stamp cards at my reach, which are usually offered to the customer when they make a purchase. I simply asked if he could stamp a card so I could come back and he replied very rude "No" in a very sassy way....I was shocked and replied why not? In my head I thought am I missing something? It took him a few seconds for him to say "I mean I could have refused you know?" Then he went on saying imagine if I had refused? And I understood he was probably joking but I don't understand why an owner of a new small business would joke around like that with new customers on their first interaction with the place....I could have definitely felt very offended and ask for my money back. Which I didn't but that's the reason I won't be returning to this place. Even aside from the whole owner to customer interaction, the taste of the latte is not worth me going back. I would much rather go to other coffee places like Jameson Brown  Coffee Roasters or Copa Vida their lattes are perfection.</review>
